<review>If you like Coffee or tea, Peets is the best place hands-down in the Nut Tree or Premium Outlets. Coffee is brewed fresh every 30 minutes, the baristas hand-pull every shot, and the warm breakfast sandwiches are a great snack when you need a little something for breakfast/between meals. We've got a huge variety of beans and teas you can try, as well as your favorite cold and blended drinks when you want something sweet. I work here, so I can't comment on the service, but I will say that we do our best to help you pick the right drink if you've never been here before. <text>I thought it would be hard to transition to a different gym because I came from a pretty awesome place. I am picky about the coaching and programming and I'm happy to say that Carson CrossFit has been successful in both. The coaches are really knowledgeable and they know what they're doing; they are organized and can control the flow of classes really well.
It's easy to say that I respect all of the coaches at Carson CrossFit. All the coaches there really want you to progressed and become the better version of yourself.
They always have different events and activities going on - this keeps it fresh and exciting! They host different in-house competitions, fun challenges, and other fun activities for family and friends. They really care about their members and constantly work to make it a better place.

<Review>5.5 years with Carson Crossfit and would not change it for a regular gym ever. I will continue here. I loved it so much that I've brought my son (now 26y,  medical school student, New York) and daughter (21y, Down Syndrome) as well, and they continued training with me ever since; my daughter always with me, 3 times/week, and my son whenever with us or on his own (crossfit, sailing).

I've started crossfit there initially in a fitness program open by the company for which I presently work, Union Pacific Railroad (UPRR), for 3.5 months. Loved it so much, lost 10 lbs and gained strength and endurance, that I've decided to continue with them, and not another program or regular gym. After the initial 3.5 months, UPRR was not decided to continue or not to pay for us at Carson Crossfit; therefore, I've paid from my won pocket and continued the workout with my kids as well. Finally, UPRR decided to pay in full crossfit sessions for all employees who wanted to enroll and, since, they paid for me and my daughter, which was great. Nevertheless, should they stop, I'd restart personal payments and continue the crossfit workout, especially at Carson Crossfit.

A few reasons:

The only routine is the group itself that shares the same workout with you, and that there is a trainer present all the time. Otherwise, exercises change every single day, which keep you motivated, active and in shape for new training opportunities

Every single routine has not only one type of exercise, but a combination of weight lifting, gymnastics and cardio - can you easily beat that?

Many times routines determine you to use your own body weight - so you start to know yourself a little better

Staff: professional, trained, pays attention to individual needs; addresses personal requests; advises all the time possible

Group: hardworking, funny, respectful, celebrates and acknowledges results

Last but not least: once a year you have the opportunity to participate in an open contest world-wide in your age group to see how well you are and/or how much more work you'd still want do, or preserve what you've gained. Last year, not being present in US, I have participated from vacation in Romania with my son in the open, and I-T W-A-S G-R-E-A-T!

Try Carson Crossfit as well! :) By the way, the picture attached is from my birthday short celebration at Carson Crossfit, after the workout.</Review><user_id>114222224572602370502</user_id></record></dataset><record>

<rating>5<//rating><Text>I have never been the biggest fan of crossfit gyms. I was introduced to this one because my old strength and conditioning gym closed down and a lot of the members gave this gym a try. I was intimidated by how everyone appeared to be more advanced than my current position, but the reason I stayed is the ambience of the gym and the coaches, owners, and athletes alike. Everyone is friendly. The coaches show great concern on your well being and fitness journey. Every time I have addressed a goal or a certain concern, the coaches go out of their way to help me get there. They always go above and beyond. I am extremely thankful for the type of family I am gaining from this gym. I have several body issues - one of the most consist one is my hip. I almost always seem to be injured and it's a little discouraging because I would have to go lighter, or sometimes it is too much and I can't always catch up with the other people in class. What I really appreciate, however, is that the coaches are always ready to help modify WODs to fit my current circumstance. They have given me pointers, addressed videos, and went well out of their way to try to resolve my consistent hip issue. It has really motivated me to work better on my form, knowing that once I have gotten that down... the strength portion will come back. During the work outs, everyone motivates another. < Review>
There are a lot of things I consider when choosing a permanent place to do workouts and I hope this gives you an idea of why I love CCF.

FRIENDLINESS:
I started coming here when my former CrossFit Gym closed, and I was skeptical that I would find comfort starting over in a new environment. I was pleasantly surprised how welcoming everyone is - I've been to many boxes where no one says hi, or acknowledges you until you say something. As soon as you walk in the door, you'll get a "what-up" or "hi" from at least one person.

COACHING:
This is why you want to go to a CrossFit Gym and growing with all the members at CCF. Coaches go over each movement and take everything step by step - they continually work on perfecting your movements and you will definitely see results in lifting by strategizing each WOD. All the coaches work on elevating their credentials to better serve the members by attending seminars, certification courses, and growing with everyone.

EQUIPMENT/SPACE:
The facility is always progressing, whether by renovation, new equipment, or having sponsors bring gear for special events. There's always something going on the calendar. There is plenty of space along with top-notch equipment that makes this a place to be proud of. Each section is geared towards a special purpose, and it never feels crowded during WODs. A welcoming lobby with snacks and recovery drinks fulfills everyone's needs after a tough workout, and it never disappoints to satisfy - I find myself getting something almost every day.

COMRADERIE:
This really makes or breaks a quality gym - by the people you see every day. Everyone is super nice and non-intimidating, which makes me want to come 5 days a week. This truly is the best hour of my day (aside from spending time with my family). Humility mixed with bumping music and max effort from each member makes a pretty awesome day.

BOTTOM LINE:
Drop in! You won't regret it!</Review>

- My wife and I left and went to the car and tried the online site, but were unable to get their appointment scheduler to open so we called....my wife told them what we wanted to do and they told us, sure - renewals and taking photos are quick, they'd be happy to do it for us, all we needed to do was come in, they'd take the photo and then help us send the forms in the correct mailer, pay the fees and we'd be done. - We did and they were really helpful. We waited off to the side and the person who came to help us checked to make sure we had the right forms ready, and we did and she took us back to take the photos. She printed them and about 5 minutes later we were done and thanking them for being so helpful.
- I was kind of amazed at how differently they were at the two offices. My other experiences at PO's has been pretty good. When we're in Middletown (Bob and his crew rock!), Rohnert Park (Always!!), Santa Rosa, Alameda - just about everywhere they're always helpful and reasonably courteous even when really busy. And they always have basic office supplies like paper to write a customer notes on, pens to write with, etc. I felt sorry for Clearlake, like I should drop off some packs of yellow stickies or something and let them know I'm a pretty good photographer myself so if they give me the correct spec's and processing information I'd be happy to free lance - or even volunteer. They do need some help to be sure and I have to give it one star if only because the USPS should stand by what they publish on their website and what they give out over the phone. Hopefully they will get the help they need to do so.
- So big prop's to Lakeport for seeing us and understanding that a renewal is much less demanding than a new one to process (a process I don't know much about as a customer) and doing us inbetween whatever other appointments they had, and doing so as if it was the easiest thing for them to do.</Text>

<review>I was just driving by this burger joint.  Then my friend said they had good burgers.  What's a GOOD burger? I thought... So instead of asking him. I drove in.
They had a full menu over the counter, i could see cars pull by their drive-thru, they didn't seem to be waiting to long... Star!  I had to ask the lady for the house specialty, she looked confused so i just went with a burger combo.
We ordered two of the same, when she rang us up the total was around $8bucks and change, cool.  As I was about to reach for my wallet to pay for my order.  She walked away...  It was the price for both combo's!... Boom! Star!  It didnt take long when she called our number. Two average sized burgers and pair of steaming hot fries, we already had our drinks.
Ok.. the fries were piping hot! Fresh out the fryer.  Burgers has noticeably fresh veggies, and a freshly cook patty I took a bite... Hmmmm.  I said "this is a good! Burger"...Star!  All in all there's nothing bad about this place, also nothing super.  That's it.

My friend wouldnt stop raving about the fountain drinks, he swore their syrup mix for the soda was unlike no other place in L.A....  IDK
So just in case he hits this post some day...Star!
